//Fun fact: This was the first boss I coded. Then, on 17/05/2016, I did a massive reformat to make it function better.

ACTOR Cirno 31154
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Cirno"
  floatspeed 8
  Speed 8
  MONSTER
  Health 1400
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 9001 //The STRONGEST mass
  MinMissileChance 160
  //MinMissileChance 3000 //Modder clearly didn't understand how this works
  //MeleeThreshold 35	//MeleeThreshold was LOWER than MeleeRange
  //MeleeRange 65		//How did the original guy even make touhou doom functional
  +NeverRespawn

  +FloorClip
  +NoGravity
  +Float
  +Boss
  +NoRadiusDMG

	CIRN A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,10,25)
	CIRN A 1 A_Look
  Idle:
    CIRN BCDEFA 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	CIRN A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_Chase
	Loop
  ChaseState:
    CIRN A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_Chase
	Loop

ACTOR CirnoIcicleFall : Cirno
{
  Tag "Cirno"
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  DropItem "CirnoNS2"
  Health 1500
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	CIRN A 0
	CIRN A 15 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
	CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_FadeIn(0.15)
  Idle:
	CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_Look
	Loop
  See:
    CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")	
	Goto Missile
  Missile:
    CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"IcicleFallAttack")
	CIRN A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6009)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6009,1,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6009,35)
    CIRN A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,3)
	CIR2 AABBCCDDEFEFEFEFGGHH 3 A_FaceTarget
    CIRN A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	CIRN A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
  IcicleFallAttack:
	CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(768,"StartIcicleFall1")
	CIRN A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360,15,0,0)
  StartIcicleFall1:
    CIRN N 10 A_FaceTarget
	CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(640,"StartIcicleFall2")

ACTOR CirnoPerfectFreeze : Cirno
{
  Tag "Cirno"
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  DropItem "None"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	CIRN A 0
	CIRN A 15 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
	CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_FadeIn(0.15)
  Idle:
	CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_Look
	Loop
  See:
    CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")	
	Goto Missile
  Missile:
    CIRN A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
    CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"PerfectFreezeAttack")
	CIRN A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6011)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6011,0,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6011,45)
    CIRN A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,4)

ACTOR CirnoDiamondBlizzard : Cirno
{
  Tag "Cirno"
  +INVULNERABLE
  Health 1800
  DropItem "None"
  Deathsound "touhou/defeat"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	CIRN A 0
	CIRN A 15 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
	CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_FadeIn(0.15)
  Idle:
	CIRN ABCDEF 3 A_Look
	Loop
  See:
    CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")	
	Goto Missile
  Missile:
    CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"DiamondBlizzardAttack")
	CIRN A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
    CIRN A 0 ACS_Execute(603,0)
	CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/pain",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	CIRN ABCDEF 3
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6012)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6012,0,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6012,45)
    CIRN A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,5)
	CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	CIR2 AABBCCDDEFEFEFEFGGHH 3 A_FaceTarget
	CIRN A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	Goto DiamondBlizzardAttack
  EndFight:
    CIRN A 0 A_Die
	Goto See

    CIRN N 35 A_FaceTarget
	CIRN A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"DBNormal")

	CIRN O 6 A_SpawnItemEx("DiamondBlizzardNormalSpawner",frandom(-32,32),frandom(-32,32),frandom(48,192),0,0,0,0,0,0)
	CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0)
	CIRN P 6 A_SpawnItemEx("DiamondBlizzardNormalSpawner",frandom(-32,32),frandom(-32,32),frandom(48,192),0,0,0,0,0,0)
	CIRN A 0 A_Wander
	CIRN A 0 A_CPosRefire
	Goto DBNormal
  DBHard:
    CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0)
	CIRN O 6 A_SpawnItemEx("DiamondBlizzardHardSpawner",frandom(-32,32),frandom(-32,32),frandom(48,192),0,0,0,0,0,0)
	CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0)
	CIRN P 6 A_SpawnItemEx("DiamondBlizzardHardSpawner",frandom(-32,32),frandom(-32,32),frandom(48,192),0,0,0,0,0,0)
	CIRN A 0 A_Wander

    CIRN A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0)

{

  Height 9
  Speed 9
  FastSpeed 6

    Loop
  Orange:
	OBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PerfectFreezeChecker",1,"StopMoving")	
    Loop
  Yellow:
	YBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PerfectFreezeChecker",1,"StopMoving")	
    Loop
  Green:
	GBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PerfectFreezeChecker",1,"StopMoving")	
    Loop
  Cyan:
	CBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PerfectFreezeChecker",1,"StopMoving")	
    Loop
  Blue:
	BBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PerfectFreezeChecker",1,"StopMoving")	
    Loop
  Violet:
	VBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PerfectFreezeChecker",1,"StopMoving")	
    Loop
  StopMoving:
    WBL2 A 175 Bright A_Stop
	WBL2 A 0 Bright A_SetAngle(frandom(0,360))
	WBL2 AAAAA 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	WBL2 AAAAAAA 5 Bright ThrustThing(angle*256/360, 3, 0, 0)
  NewSpawn:
	WBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	Loop
  Death:
    WBL2 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}
